<div id="review_34737198" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/34737198" />
    <a title="Lisa Lap" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/174487-lisa-lap"><img alt="Lisa Lap" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1183751908p2/174487.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/34737198?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa Lap" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa Lap" href="/user/show/174487-lisa-lap">Lisa Lap</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/174487-lisa-lap?shelf=paranormalromance">paranormalromance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/174487-lisa-lap?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/174487-lisa-lap?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/174487-lisa-lap?shelf=booksireadoverandover">booksireadoverandover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/174487-lisa-lap?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer34737198" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1614285697069149313">Finally Noah gets an imprinted mate! The demon king has needed one for a long while now and I was so relieved for him that he finally found Kestra. However, Noah became a smaller version of himself because of his fear of losing her. Noah, for me, has always been larger than life - even more so than the others. By seeing Kestra's death - which he then circumvents to save her - he sort of folded in on himself to me. He withheld so many facets of his personality to not scare Kestra off that I wante</span>
  <span id="freeText1614285697069149313" style="display:none">Finally Noah gets an imprinted mate! The demon king has needed one for a long while now and I was so relieved for him that he finally found Kestra. However, Noah became a smaller version of himself because of his fear of losing her. Noah, for me, has always been larger than life - even more so than the others. By seeing Kestra's death - which he then circumvents to save her - he sort of folded in on himself to me. He withheld so many facets of his personality to not scare Kestra off that I wanted to scream in frustration. When Legna and Bella both told him to just be himself - and that anyone he has ever loved has never turned away from him he finally became NOAH again. Even more frustrating was to then realize that Kestra was aware of how Noah was holding himself back the entire time. I felt it wasted a lot of time that could have been put to better use. Damn Noah and his stubborn spirit. Nice little twist to have the fairy tale be the story of his parents. <br /><br />I think what happened to Kestra was horrible, but I also think the story of how what happened to her turned her into a marine then a merc was never really fleshed out. So she is tactician and a warrior and displays incredible abilities once she begins emerging as a druid... like we had any doubt Noah's mate would have these qualities? I wish we knew more about the why instead of just getting the deets. Still there was no denying the chemistry between Kestra and Noah was red hot as is should be for the Fire Demon King.<br /><br />The side stories were a little distracting at first because they weren't picking up from where Ruth and Nico left off their rebellion. The "threat" this time was from rebelling factions displeased over the marriage of Damien and Syreena. I like how we get to see characters from previous books but in this case it felt a little disconnected. Damien's fears are well founded that his people are not eager to accept what was previously taboo - his marriage to Syreena. The leap for rebelling vampires to try absorbing other Nightwalker powers wasn't a big one as of course there will be corrupt Nightwalkers. Hello - RUTH - why hasn't she figured this out and where was she throughout this book?<br /><br />I realize a lot of the "side stories" in this book were to set up the next story arc but I felt it jumped around a little more than previous books. I'm curious to see where it goes from here, although it will be a while and it will be with a Nightwalker species not really talked about much - Shadowdwellers. We'll see. I know I'll keep reading and I hope Noah and Kestra's story gets a little more play in the future.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1614285697069149313" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Ally" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/990135-ally"><img alt="Ally" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1205413869p2/990135.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/205461824?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ally" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ally" href="/user/show/990135-ally">Ally</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/990135-ally?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/990135-ally?shelf=2011">2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/990135-ally?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer205461824" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17901885847517920585">Paranormal Romance<br/>Nightwalkers #5<br/>1st September 2008<br/>Kindle<br/>2 Stars<br/>As Demon King, Noah is dedicated to protecting his kind from their human and Nightwalker enemies. Yet for six months he has struggled with vivid dreams that threaten his very sanity. Every night he's tormented by images of a woman both achingly real and tantalisingly beyond his grasp. And his bone-deep need leaves him no choice but to force her to leave the life she's known and enter a world beyond her imagining.Every day, Kestra ri</span>
  <span id="freeText17901885847517920585" style="display:none">Paranormal Romance<br />Nightwalkers #5<br />1st September 2008<br />Kindle<br />2 Stars<br />As Demon King, Noah is dedicated to protecting his kind from their human and Nightwalker enemies. Yet for six months he has struggled with vivid dreams that threaten his very sanity. Every night he's tormented by images of a woman both achingly real and tantalisingly beyond his grasp. And his bone-deep need leaves him no choice but to force her to leave the life she's known and enter a world beyond her imagining.Every day, Kestra risks her life in perilous missions that veer just shy of the law, but she instinctively knows that the imposingly sensual figure before her is a danger unlike any she's ever faced. Kestra has sworn never to trust or need another man, but Noah's lightest touch scorches her with fevered desire, branding her as his mate, blinding them both to the terrifying truth. For within ranks of their own people lies an adversary growing in number and power. And nothing and no one will be safe again.<br /><br />Well... what can I say? To be blunt and to the point I really didn’t like Noah. It just didn’t work for me at all and I felt so let down when reading Noah. For starters the three previous books that I’ve read in the series (yes I missed out book 3 and read the others) Noah comes off as a truly great and interesting character and I know that when the characters are to meet their mates there’s all that funny business with the moon and sending them mad twice a year and them acting out of character but not only did Noah seem out of character he seemed like a different character all together! Which didn’t work for me and how the heroine, Kestra managed to accept everything in the Nightwalker world didn’t work for me and I struggled to accept the storyline. Really this would have been a total DNF for me except that Noah provided us with lots of information about the other characters from previous books and the next book to come that I had to stick with it just to find out what would happen with them. However, I may end up reading Adam which is out 25th October but only because Jasmine has intrigued me on and off throughout the series but I’m still undecided if I want to give this series a third try!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17901885847517920585" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_296006689" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/296006689" />
    <a title="Drucilla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5476796-drucilla"><img alt="Drucilla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305917933p2/5476796.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/296006689?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Drucilla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Drucilla" href="/user/show/5476796-drucilla">Drucilla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5476796-drucilla?shelf=f">f</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer296006689" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14355390729329794498">I was really looking forward to Noah's book, but I was very disappointed. This series seems to be going quickly downhill. What started out as a very cool fantasy/paranormal romance series is quickly turning into your standard, no surprises paranormal romance. Ruth and Nico aren't in this book at all and as the main villains of the series, I don't know why they weren't. The plot of the rogue vampires <i>did</i> fit well considering what happened in the previous book, but it just didn't have enough impor</span>
  <span id="freeText14355390729329794498" style="display:none">I was really looking forward to Noah's book, but I was very disappointed. This series seems to be going quickly downhill. What started out as a very cool fantasy/paranormal romance series is quickly turning into your standard, no surprises paranormal romance. Ruth and Nico aren't in this book at all and as the main villains of the series, I don't know why they weren't. The plot of the rogue vampires <i>did</i> fit well considering what happened in the previous book, but it just didn't have enough importance to be the main plot. I know you're probably thinking, "The romance is the main plot" and in this case, you'd be right. See, in the previous books the romance and plot were divided evenly, but starting in <i>Damien</i> the books start to shift focus more heavily to the romance side. It's not a big problem in <i>Damien</i>, but it is in this book. The author sacrifices plot and world building for the romance. Like I said, a standard, no suprises paranormal romance.<br /><br />Now for the characters. I didn't really like Kestra. She was too yo-yo for me and way too confrontational. Perhaps the most disappointment I experienced with this book was Noah, himself. I really liked him in the previous books, but he seems <i>so</i> different in this one. I did like that the author finally showed the demon madness that's been discussed in every previous book and, not only that, she had Noah be the maddened one. It really helped shape his character better. Unfortunately, Noah's an a*hole throughout most of the book. Most of the characters show up in this book and whereas I liked when it was done in the previous books, in <i>Noah</i> it's just too much. Too many characters show up and contribute nothing to the plot. With this book clocking in at close to 500 pages, many of these random character interruptions could have been taken out. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14355390729329794498" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781420107265" href="/book/show/8603466-noah">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=smexy-erotica">smexy-erotica</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer228238629" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13776710965599963788">3.5stars<br/>For this installment it's past time for Demon king, Noah, to find his mate. After 650 years of waiting, including three of those where his nearest and dearest have found their HEA's, Noah is beginning to lose his grip on reality which is causing his friends a bit of consternation. Noah's dreams of his future mate Kestra, a contract killer, has him wanting to seek assistance from Corrine if he can get over his fear of his possible future with Kestra. But due to Kestra's lifestyle and Noah</span>
  <span id="freeText13776710965599963788" style="display:none">3.5stars<br />For this installment it's past time for Demon king, Noah, to find his mate. After 650 years of waiting, including three of those where his nearest and dearest have found their HEA's, Noah is beginning to lose his grip on reality which is causing his friends a bit of consternation. Noah's dreams of his future mate Kestra, a contract killer, has him wanting to seek assistance from Corrine if he can get over his fear of his possible future with Kestra. But due to Kestra's lifestyle and Noah's delay in seeking her he has to go extraordinary measure to find his own HEA. <br />I liked Kestra's warrior take-no-prisoners attitude and thought she was a fully articulated character when she first appeared but then she changed and just became annoying. Noah, though still likeable enough for me was different than his character was originally introduced and he seemed to have lost the power of speech because he spent so much time chuckling which diminished him somewhat for me when he had previously been rather straightforward.<br /> Once again I found this installment so overly descriptive it distracted from the plot, but was paced well enough with enough familiar characters to keep me reading. The story in the middle was distracting as well and in my opinion helped underscore the uneven writing style. Unfortunately I still want to like this series so much more than I do and think the idea of this series is so much better than the reality of it. In any event this entry was much more to my taste than the previous installment <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2327958.Damien__Nightwalkers___4_" title="Damien (Nightwalkers, #4) by Jacquelyn Frank" rel="nofollow noopener">Damien</a>.<br /></span>

<div id="review_207437053" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/207437053" />
    <a title="Kasey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2878675-kasey"><img alt="Kasey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1298899891p2/2878675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/207437053?book_show_action=true">Sep 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kasey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kasey" href="/user/show/2878675-kasey">Kasey</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2878675-kasey?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2878675-kasey?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2878675-kasey?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2878675-kasey?shelf=shifters-weres">shifters-weres</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2878675-kasey?shelf=demons-gods-or-goddess">demons-gods-or-goddess</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer207437053" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15972365161885558443">So glad to finally get Noah's story. I've really enjoyed getting to know him throughout the series. I absolutely loved Kes when this story started. She was a strong heroine and was just what Noah needed in a mate. She could take care of herself and didn't make any bones about it. She had her own rough history and had a lot to get over and I appreciate that. If I was rating this book on just the romance of Noah and Kes I would give it four stars. Five if it wasn't for the long drawn out wait for </span>
  <span id="freeText15972365161885558443" style="display:none">So glad to finally get Noah's story. I've really enjoyed getting to know him throughout the series. I absolutely loved Kes when this story started. She was a strong heroine and was just what Noah needed in a mate. She could take care of herself and didn't make any bones about it. She had her own rough history and had a lot to get over and I appreciate that. If I was rating this book on just the romance of Noah and Kes I would give it four stars. Five if it wasn't for the long drawn out wait for them to get past the problems between them close to the end. It just didn't flow well for me and to be honest made me want to slap both of them Kes the most. The woman was stubborn to the end :)<br /><br />But this story is number five in a series and there has been a subplot going on throughout the series and while I could understand how the bad guys came about and their coming around was pretty natural. The problem is for four books we have had a demoness named Ruth leading the big bad against the nightwalkers and we had no sign of her or explanation to what is going on with her. She was mentioned briefly in passing and that was it. To top it off this was originally the last book so I am glad to know Frank has decided to add a book to the series and I have hopes that all my questions will be answered there. Still not a fan of Jasmine, but look forward to reading her story regardless. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15972365161885558443" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('tIx+HIyT7xCZBVgnwiU+As/vu5rPX57u3luQWQZf28eqs74nb+jcUMumpMQtuj6oA2qS/bugNof4TpklnVBU3Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('B8IYxwVaUNkU4g8TR3fMHD9WbtTGw1YcgQ8UbMRGcWsZ/dj85iFjmUZB8/Co6My289NHs7I8/nWnGh0QX0n+cQ==')})
  }

And more interested in saving her skin than draining it.\n\nEtienne has been an Immortal Guardian for two hundred years--long enough to know that Krysta is special.
